      </div>
      <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Sanuwave announces Q1 2023 financial results</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE Health, Inc.</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">EDEN PRAIRIE, MN, May 12, 2023</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE Health, Inc. (OTCQB: SNWV), a leading provider of next-generation FDA-approved wound care products, today announced 1st quarter 2023 results.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">For the three-months ended March 31, 2023:</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="za79cd29283dd42e0a15b05ceec3e2b92" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Revenues increased 18% to $3.8 million for Q1 2023 versus $3.2 million for the same period last year. This growth falls within the guidance range of 14-20%, provided on the prior conference call.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z72958f560ef54eef9bcc9ca0acf2fffe" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">UltraMist<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup> systems sold increased 12% to 28 for Q1 2023, versus 25 systems for the same period last year.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z6f1a4acb02dd4e26bc27a002566fdda1" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">UltraMist<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">&#174;</sup> applicator cases sold increased 18% to 3,641, versus 3,093 applicator cases for the same period last year.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z2a3a64140f1241c29332738e2049c64d" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Gross margin as a percentage of revenue decreased for the three months ended March 31, 2023, to 67% from 72% for the same period last year.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z239d6405c1754b719c396a179f7a19cb" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Operating loss totaled $2.0 million for the three months ended March 31, 2023, which was flat compared to the same period last year.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z30219a0470904669be81494b18e8bf81" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <tr>
            <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
            </td>
            <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
            <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
              <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">We anticipate second quarter revenue growth to fall within a range of 15-25%.</div>
            </td>
          </tr>

      </table>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div>
        <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Mr. Kevin Richardson, CEO, stated, &#8220;We are very pleased with the strong interest we observed from customers at the three conferences we attended.&#160; The Third Annual
          Leaders in Wound Healing Conference in New Orleans, the Symposium on Advanced Wood Care Spring (SAWC Spring) in National Harbor, MD, and EWMA 2023 Symposium in Milan, Italy. <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 30, 32);">
            These conferences were an </font>ideal platform for us to showcase our innovative non-invasive, regenerative medicine solutions for the treatment of chronic wounds.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE Health is committed to advancing the field of regenerative medicine and improving patient care. The company's groundbreaking technology has been shown to
          accelerate the healing of chronic wounds, leading to improved patient outcomes and reduced healthcare costs."</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Subsequent to the end of the quarter, the company raised an additional approximately $1.2 million in order to maximize flexibility around sales hiring and inventory
        build.&#160; Terms were consistent with the previous financing. This cash is not reflected in the Q1 statements.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div class="BRPFPageBreakArea" style="clear: both; margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 10pt;">
        <div class="BRPFPageBreak" style="page-break-after: always;">

      <div>
        <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Guidance</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Company has continued to have constrained inventory supply during Q1 2023. Despite this, we anticipate revenue growth of approximately 15% to 25% during Q2 2023,
          compared to Q2 2022. The company believes that supply is further improving and that we will observe continued increase in revenue growth in Q2 2023.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">As previously announced a business update will occur via conference call on May 12, 2022.&#160; Materials for the conference call at 9:00 a.m. EST are included on the company
        website,<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"> <u>www.sanuwave.com/investors</u></font>.</div>

      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">About SANUWAVE</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE Health is focused on the research, development, and commercialization of its patented, non-invasive and biological response-activating medical systems for the
        repair and regeneration of skin, musculoskeletal tissue, and vascular structures.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE&#8217;s end-to-end wound care portfolio of regenerative medicine products and product candidates help restore the body&#8217;s normal healing processes. SANUWAVE applies and
        researches its patented energy transfer technologies in wound healing, orthopedic/spine, aesthetic/cosmetic, and cardiac/endovascular conditions.</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
